(*****************************************************************

 Limits in self enriched categories

 Self enriched categories inherit their limits from the
 underlying category. In addition, self enriched categories always
 have powers, and these are given by the internal hom.

 Contents
 1. Terminal object
 2. Binary products
 3. Equalizers
 4. Powers
 5. Type indexed products

 *****************************************************************)
Require Import UniMath.Foundations.All.

[notation-overridden,parsing,default]

[notation-overridden,parsing,default]

Local Open Scope cat.
Local Open Scope moncat.
Import MonoidalNotations.

Opaque sym_mon_braiding.

Section SelfEnrichmentLimits.
  Context (V : sym_mon_closed_cat).

  (**
   1. Terminal object
   *)
  Section SelfEnrichmentTerminal.
    Context (v : V)
            (Hv : isTerminal V v).

    
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
v: V
Hv: isTerminal V v
is_terminal_enriched (self_enrichment V) v

    
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
v: V
Hv: isTerminal V v
is_terminal_enriched (self_enrichment V) v

      
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
v: V
Hv: isTerminal V v
∏ w y : V, V ⟦ w, self_enrichment V ⦃ y, v ⦄ ⟧
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
v: V
Hv: isTerminal V v
∏ (w y : V)
(f g : V ⟦ w, self_enrichment V ⦃ y, v ⦄ ⟧), f = g

      
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
v: V
Hv: isTerminal V v
∏ w y : V, V ⟦ w, self_enrichment V ⦃ y, v ⦄ ⟧
 exact (λ _ _, internal_lam (TerminalArrow (_ ,, Hv) _)).
      
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
v: V
Hv: isTerminal V v
∏ (w y : V)
(f g : V ⟦ w, self_enrichment V ⦃ y, v ⦄ ⟧), f = g
 abstract
          (cbn ;
           intros w y f g ;
           use internal_funext ;
           intros a h ;
           apply (@TerminalArrowEq _ (v ,, Hv))).
    Defined.
  End SelfEnrichmentTerminal.

  Definition self_enrichment_terminal
             (HV : Terminal V)
    : terminal_enriched (self_enrichment V)
    := pr1 HV ,, self_enrichment_is_terminal_enriched _ (pr2 HV).

  (**
   2. Binary products
   *)
  Section SelfEnrichmentProduct.
    Context {v₁ v₂ w : V}
            (π₁ : w --> v₁)
            (π₂ : w --> v₂)
            (H : isBinProduct _ _ _ _ π₁ π₂).

    Let prod : BinProduct V v₁ v₂ := make_BinProduct _ _ _ _ _ _ H.

    Definition self_enrichment_binary_product_pr1
      : I_{V} --> w ⊸ v₁
      := internal_lam (mon_lunitor _ · π₁).

    Definition self_enrichment_binary_product_pr2
      : I_{V} --> w ⊸ v₂
      := internal_lam (mon_lunitor _ · π₂).

    
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
v₁, v₂, w: V
π₁: V ⟦ w, v₁ ⟧
π₂: V ⟦ w, v₂ ⟧
H: isBinProduct V v₁ v₂ w π₁ π₂
prod:= make_BinProduct V v₁ v₂ w π₁ π₂ H: BinProduct V v₁ v₂
enriched_binary_prod_cone (self_enrichment V) v₁ v₂

    
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
v₁, v₂, w: V
π₁: V ⟦ w, v₁ ⟧
π₂: V ⟦ w, v₂ ⟧
H: isBinProduct V v₁ v₂ w π₁ π₂
prod:= make_BinProduct V v₁ v₂ w π₁ π₂ H: BinProduct V v₁ v₂
enriched_binary_prod_cone (self_enrichment V) v₁ v₂

      
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
v₁, v₂, w: V
π₁: V ⟦ w, v₁ ⟧
π₂: V ⟦ w, v₂ ⟧
H: isBinProduct V v₁ v₂ w π₁ π₂
prod:= make_BinProduct V v₁ v₂ w π₁ π₂ H: BinProduct V v₁ v₂
V
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
v₁, v₂, w: V
π₁: V ⟦ w, v₁ ⟧
π₂: V ⟦ w, v₂ ⟧
H: isBinProduct V v₁ v₂ w π₁ π₂
prod:= make_BinProduct V v₁ v₂ w π₁ π₂ H: BinProduct V v₁ v₂
V ⟦ I_{ V}, self_enrichment V ⦃ ?a, v₁ ⦄ ⟧
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
v₁, v₂, w: V
π₁: V ⟦ w, v₁ ⟧
π₂: V ⟦ w, v₂ ⟧
H: isBinProduct V v₁ v₂ w π₁ π₂
prod:= make_BinProduct V v₁ v₂ w π₁ π₂ H: BinProduct V v₁ v₂
V ⟦ I_{ V}, self_enrichment V ⦃ ?a, v₂ ⦄ ⟧

      
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
v₁, v₂, w: V
π₁: V ⟦ w, v₁ ⟧
π₂: V ⟦ w, v₂ ⟧
H: isBinProduct V v₁ v₂ w π₁ π₂
prod:= make_BinProduct V v₁ v₂ w π₁ π₂ H: BinProduct V v₁ v₂
V
 exact w.
      
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
v₁, v₂, w: V
π₁: V ⟦ w, v₁ ⟧
π₂: V ⟦ w, v₂ ⟧
H: isBinProduct V v₁ v₂ w π₁ π₂
prod:= make_BinProduct V v₁ v₂ w π₁ π₂ H: BinProduct V v₁ v₂
V ⟦ I_{ V}, self_enrichment V ⦃ w, v₁ ⦄ ⟧
 exact self_enrichment_binary_product_pr1.
      
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
v₁, v₂, w: V
π₁: V ⟦ w, v₁ ⟧
π₂: V ⟦ w, v₂ ⟧
H: isBinProduct V v₁ v₂ w π₁ π₂
prod:= make_BinProduct V v₁ v₂ w π₁ π₂ H: BinProduct V v₁ v₂
V ⟦ I_{ V}, self_enrichment V ⦃ w, v₂ ⦄ ⟧
 exact self_enrichment_binary_product_pr2.
    Defined.

    Definition self_enrichment_pair
               {a b : V}
               (f : a --> b ⊸ v₁)
               (g : a --> b ⊸ v₂)
      : a --> b ⊸ w
      := internal_lam
           (BinProductArrow
              V
              prod
              (f #⊗ identity _ · internal_eval _ _)
              (g #⊗ identity _ · internal_eval _ _)).

    
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
v₁, v₂, w: V
π₁: V ⟦ w, v₁ ⟧
π₂: V ⟦ w, v₂ ⟧
H: isBinProduct V v₁ v₂ w π₁ π₂
prod:= make_BinProduct V v₁ v₂ w π₁ π₂ H: BinProduct V v₁ v₂
a, b: V
f: V ⟦ a, b ⊸ v₁ ⟧
g: V ⟦ a, b ⊸ v₂ ⟧
self_enrichment_pair f g
· postcomp_arr (self_enrichment V) b
    (internal_to_arr
       self_enrichment_binary_product_pr1) = f

    
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
v₁, v₂, w: V
π₁: V ⟦ w, v₁ ⟧
π₂: V ⟦ w, v₂ ⟧
H: isBinProduct V v₁ v₂ w π₁ π₂

· postcomp_arr (self_enrichment V) b
    (internal_to_arr
       self_enrichment_binary_product_pr1) = f

· internal_lam
    (internal_eval b w

V: sym_mon_closed_cat
v₁, v₂, w: V
π₁: V ⟦ w, v₁ ⟧
π₂: V ⟦ w, v₂ ⟧
H: isBinProduct V v₁ v₂ w π₁ π₂

a, b: V
f: V ⟦ a, b ⊸ v₁ ⟧
g: V ⟦ a, b ⊸ v₂ ⟧
∏ (a0 : V) (h : V ⟦ a0, b ⟧),
(self_enrichment_pair f g
 · internal_lam
     (internal_eval b w
      · internal_to_arr
          self_enrichment_binary_product_pr1)) #⊗ h
· internal_eval b v₁ = f #⊗ h · internal_eval b v₁

V: sym_mon_closed_cat

    Definition pair_fun_pr1
               {a b : V}
               (φ : a --> b ⊸ w)
      : a --> b ⊸ v₁
      := φ · postcomp_arr
               (self_enrichment V)
               _
               (internal_to_arr self_enrichment_binary_product_pr1).

    Definition pair_fun_pr2
               {a b : V}
               (φ : a --> b ⊸ w)
      : a --> b ⊸ v₂
      := φ · postcomp_arr
               (self_enrichment V)
               _
               (internal_to_arr self_enrichment_binary_product_pr2).

π₂: V ⟦ w, v₂ ⟧
H: isBinProduct V v₁ v₂ w π₁ π₂
prod:= make_BinProduct V v₁ v₂ w π₁ π₂ H: BinProduct V v₁ v₂
a, b: V
φ, ψ: V ⟦ a, b ⊸ w ⟧
p₁: pair_fun_pr1 φ = pair_fun_pr1 ψ
p₂: pair_fun_pr2 φ = pair_fun_pr2 ψ
φ = ψ

p₂: pair_fun_pr2 φ = pair_fun_pr2 ψ

pair_fun_pr1 ψ #⊗ h · internal_eval b v₁ =
pair_fun_pr1 ψ #⊗ h · internal_eval b v₁

        apply idpath.
      
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
v₁, v₂, w: V
π₁: V ⟦ w, v₁ ⟧

prod:= make_BinProduct V v₁ v₂ w π₁ π₂ H: BinProduct V v₁ v₂

V: sym_mon_closed_cat
v₁, v₂, w: V
π₁: V ⟦ w, v₁ ⟧
π₂: V ⟦ w, v₂ ⟧
H: isBinProduct V v₁ v₂ w π₁ π₂
prod:= make_BinProduct V v₁ v₂ w π₁ π₂ H: BinProduct V v₁ v₂
a, b: V
φ, ψ: V ⟦ a, b ⊸ w ⟧
p₁: pair_fun_pr1 φ = pair_fun_pr1 ψ
p₂: pair_fun_pr2 φ = pair_fun_pr2 ψ
c: V
h: V ⟦ c, b ⟧
pair_fun_pr2 φ #⊗ h · internal_eval b v₂ =
pair_fun_pr2 ψ #⊗ h · internal_eval b v₂

        
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
v₁, v₂, w: V
π₁: V ⟦ w, v₁ ⟧
π₂: V ⟦ w, v₂ ⟧
H: isBinProduct V v₁ v₂ w π₁ π₂
prod:= make_BinProduct V v₁ v₂ w π₁ π₂ H: BinProduct V v₁ v₂
a, b: V
φ, ψ: V ⟦ a, b ⊸ w ⟧
p₁: pair_fun_pr1 φ = pair_fun_pr1 ψ
p₂: pair_fun_pr2 φ = pair_fun_pr2 ψ
c: V
h: V ⟦ c, b ⟧
pair_fun_pr2 ψ #⊗ h · internal_eval b v₂ =
pair_fun_pr2 ψ #⊗ h · internal_eval b v₂

        apply idpath.
    Qed.
  End SelfEnrichmentProduct.

· postcomp_arr (self_enrichment V) w0
    (enriched_prod_cone_pr1 (self_enrichment V) v₁ v₂
       (self_enrichment_binary_products_cone π₁ π₂)) =

      self_enrichment V ⦃ w0,

       (self_enrichment_binary_products_cone π₁ π₂)) =

       (self_enrichment_binary_products_cone π₁ π₂))
→ φ₁
  · postcomp_arr (self_enrichment V) w0
      (enriched_prod_cone_pr2 (self_enrichment V) v₁
         v₂
         (self_enrichment_binary_products_cone π₁ π₂)) =
  φ₂
  · postcomp_arr (self_enrichment V) w0
      (enriched_prod_cone_pr2 (self_enrichment V) v₁
         v₂
         (self_enrichment_binary_products_cone π₁ π₂))
  → φ₁ = φ₂

PV: BinProducts V

π₂:= BinProductPr2 V (PV v₁ v₂) : V ⟦ w, v₂ ⟧: V ⟦ w, v₂ ⟧
H:= pr2 (PV v₁ v₂) : isBinProduct V v₁ v₂ w π₁ π₂: isBinProduct V v₁ v₂ w π₁ π₂
∏ w0 v : V,
V ⟦ v, self_enrichment V ⦃ w0, v₁ ⦄ ⟧
→ V ⟦ v, self_enrichment V ⦃ w0, v₂ ⦄ ⟧
  → V ⟦ v,
    self_enrichment V ⦃ w0,
    self_enrichment_binary_products_cone π₁ π₂ ⦄ ⟧
 exact (λ _ _ f g, self_enrichment_pair π₁ π₂ H f g).
      
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
PV: BinProducts V
v₁, v₂: V
w:= PV v₁ v₂ : V: V
π₁:= BinProductPr1 V (PV v₁ v₂) : V ⟦ w, v₁ ⟧: V ⟦ w, v₁ ⟧
π₂:= BinProductPr2 V (PV v₁ v₂) : V ⟦ w, v₂ ⟧: V ⟦ w, v₂ ⟧
H:= pr2 (PV v₁ v₂) : isBinProduct V v₁ v₂ w π₁ π₂: isBinProduct V v₁ v₂ w π₁ π₂
∏ (w0 v : V)
(f : V ⟦ v, self_enrichment V ⦃ w0, v₁ ⦄ ⟧)
(g : V ⟦ v, self_enrichment V ⦃ w0, v₂ ⦄ ⟧),
(λ (w1 v0 : V)
 (f0 : V ⟦ v0, self_enrichment V ⦃ w1, v₁ ⦄ ⟧)
 (g0 : V ⟦ v0, self_enrichment V ⦃ w1, v₂ ⦄ ⟧),
 self_enrichment_pair π₁ π₂ H f0 g0) w0 v f g
· postcomp_arr (self_enrichment V) w0
    (enriched_prod_cone_pr1 (self_enrichment V) v₁ v₂
       (self_enrichment_binary_products_cone π₁ π₂)) =
f
 exact (λ _ _ f g, self_enrichment_pair_pr1 π₁ π₂ H f g).
      
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
PV: BinProducts V
v₁, v₂: V
w:= PV v₁ v₂ : V: V
π₁:= BinProductPr1 V (PV v₁ v₂) : V ⟦ w, v₁ ⟧: V ⟦ w, v₁ ⟧
π₂:= BinProductPr2 V (PV v₁ v₂) : V ⟦ w, v₂ ⟧: V ⟦ w, v₂ ⟧
H:= pr2 (PV v₁ v₂) : isBinProduct V v₁ v₂ w π₁ π₂: isBinProduct V v₁ v₂ w π₁ π₂
∏ (w0 v : V)
(f : V ⟦ v, self_enrichment V ⦃ w0, v₁ ⦄ ⟧)
(g : V ⟦ v, self_enrichment V ⦃ w0, v₂ ⦄ ⟧),
(λ (w1 v0 : V)
 (f0 : V ⟦ v0, self_enrichment V ⦃ w1, v₁ ⦄ ⟧)
 (g0 : V ⟦ v0, self_enrichment V ⦃ w1, v₂ ⦄ ⟧),
 self_enrichment_pair π₁ π₂ H f0 g0) w0 v f g
· postcomp_arr (self_enrichment V) w0
    (enriched_prod_cone_pr2 (self_enrichment V) v₁ v₂
       (self_enrichment_binary_products_cone π₁ π₂)) =
g
 exact (λ _ _ f g, self_enrichment_pair_pr2 π₁ π₂ H f g).
      
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
PV: BinProducts V
v₁, v₂: V
w:= PV v₁ v₂ : V: V
π₁:= BinProductPr1 V (PV v₁ v₂) : V ⟦ w, v₁ ⟧: V ⟦ w, v₁ ⟧
π₂:= BinProductPr2 V (PV v₁ v₂) : V ⟦ w, v₂ ⟧: V ⟦ w, v₂ ⟧
H:= pr2 (PV v₁ v₂) : isBinProduct V v₁ v₂ w π₁ π₂: isBinProduct V v₁ v₂ w π₁ π₂
∏ (w0 v : V)
(φ₁
 φ₂ : V ⟦ v,
      self_enrichment V ⦃ w0,
      self_enrichment_binary_products_cone π₁ π₂ ⦄ ⟧),
φ₁
· postcomp_arr (self_enrichment V) w0
    (enriched_prod_cone_pr1 (self_enrichment V) v₁ v₂
       (self_enrichment_binary_products_cone π₁ π₂)) =
φ₂
· postcomp_arr (self_enrichment V) w0
    (enriched_prod_cone_pr1 (self_enrichment V) v₁ v₂
       (self_enrichment_binary_products_cone π₁ π₂))
→ φ₁
  · postcomp_arr (self_enrichment V) w0
      (enriched_prod_cone_pr2 (self_enrichment V) v₁
         v₂
         (self_enrichment_binary_products_cone π₁ π₂)) =
  φ₂
  · postcomp_arr (self_enrichment V) w0
      (enriched_prod_cone_pr2 (self_enrichment V) v₁
         v₂
         (self_enrichment_binary_products_cone π₁ π₂))
  → φ₁ = φ₂
 exact (λ _ _ f g, self_enrichment_pair_eq π₁ π₂ H f g).
  Defined.

  (**
   3. Equalizers
   *)
  Section SelfEnrichmentEqualizer.
    Context {v₁ v₂ e : V}
            {f g : v₁ --> v₂}
            (p : e --> v₁)
            (pfg : p · f = p · g)
            (H : isEqualizer f g p pfg).

    Let Eq : Equalizer f g := make_Equalizer _ _ _ _ H.

pfg: p · f = p · g
H: isEqualizer f g p pfg
Eq:= make_Equalizer f g p pfg H: Equalizer f g
∏ (w v : V)
(h₁
 h₂ : V ⟦ v,
      self_enrichment V ⦃ w,
      self_enrichment_equalizer_cone ⦄ ⟧),
h₁
· postcomp_arr (self_enrichment V) w
    (enriched_equalizer_cone_pr (self_enrichment V) f
       g self_enrichment_equalizer_cone) =
h₂
· postcomp_arr (self_enrichment V) w
    (enriched_equalizer_cone_pr (self_enrichment V) f
       g self_enrichment_equalizer_cone) → h₁ = h₂
 exact (λ _ _ h₁ h₂ q, self_enrichment_equalizer_eq h₁ h₂ q).
      
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
v₁, v₂, e: V
f, g: V ⟦ v₁, v₂ ⟧
p: V ⟦ e, v₁ ⟧
pfg: p · f = p · g
H: isEqualizer f g p pfg
Eq:= make_Equalizer f g p pfg H: Equalizer f g
∏ (w v : V)
(h : V ⟦ v, self_enrichment V ⦃ w, v₁ ⦄ ⟧),
h · postcomp_arr (self_enrichment V) w f =
h · postcomp_arr (self_enrichment V) w g
→ V ⟦ v,
  self_enrichment V ⦃ w,
  self_enrichment_equalizer_cone ⦄ ⟧
 exact (λ _ _ h q, self_enrichment_equalizer_arr h q).
      
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
v₁, v₂, e: V
f, g: V ⟦ v₁, v₂ ⟧
p: V ⟦ e, v₁ ⟧
pfg: p · f = p · g
H: isEqualizer f g p pfg
Eq:= make_Equalizer f g p pfg H: Equalizer f g
∏ (w v : V) (h : V ⟦ v, self_enrichment V ⦃ w, v₁ ⦄ ⟧)
(q : h · postcomp_arr (self_enrichment V) w f =
     h · postcomp_arr (self_enrichment V) w g),
(λ (w0 v0 : V)
 (h0 : V ⟦ v0, self_enrichment V ⦃ w0, v₁ ⦄ ⟧)
 (q0 : h0 · postcomp_arr (self_enrichment V) w0 f =
       h0 · postcomp_arr (self_enrichment V) w0 g),
 self_enrichment_equalizer_arr h0 q0) w v h q
· postcomp_arr (self_enrichment V) w
    (enriched_equalizer_cone_pr (self_enrichment V) f
       g self_enrichment_equalizer_cone) = h
 exact (λ _ _ h q, self_enrichment_equalizer_arr_pr h q).
    Defined.
  End SelfEnrichmentEqualizer.

  
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
EV: Equalizers V
enrichment_equalizers (self_enrichment V)

  
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
EV: Equalizers V
enrichment_equalizers (self_enrichment V)

    
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
EV: Equalizers V
v₁, v₂: V
f, g: V ⟦ v₁, v₂ ⟧
∑ a : enriched_equalizer_cone (self_enrichment V) f g,
is_equalizer_enriched (self_enrichment V) f g a

    
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
EV: Equalizers V
v₁, v₂: V
f, g: V ⟦ v₁, v₂ ⟧
e:= EV v₁ v₂ f g : V: V
∑ a : enriched_equalizer_cone (self_enrichment V) f g,
is_equalizer_enriched (self_enrichment V) f g a

    
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
EV: Equalizers V
v₁, v₂: V
f, g: V ⟦ v₁, v₂ ⟧
e:= EV v₁ v₂ f g : V: V
p:= EqualizerArrow (EV v₁ v₂ f g) : V ⟦ e, v₁ ⟧: V ⟦ e, v₁ ⟧
∑ a : enriched_equalizer_cone (self_enrichment V) f g,
is_equalizer_enriched (self_enrichment V) f g a

    
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
EV: Equalizers V
v₁, v₂: V
f, g: V ⟦ v₁, v₂ ⟧
e:= EV v₁ v₂ f g : V: V
p:= EqualizerArrow (EV v₁ v₂ f g) : V ⟦ e, v₁ ⟧: V ⟦ e, v₁ ⟧
pfg:= EqualizerEqAr (EV v₁ v₂ f g) : p · f = p · g: p · f = p · g
∑ a : enriched_equalizer_cone (self_enrichment V) f g,
is_equalizer_enriched (self_enrichment V) f g a

    
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
EV: Equalizers V
v₁, v₂: V
f, g: V ⟦ v₁, v₂ ⟧
e:= EV v₁ v₂ f g : V: V
p:= EqualizerArrow (EV v₁ v₂ f g) : V ⟦ e, v₁ ⟧: V ⟦ e, v₁ ⟧
pfg:= EqualizerEqAr (EV v₁ v₂ f g) : p · f = p · g: p · f = p · g
H:= pr22 (EV v₁ v₂ f g) : isEqualizer f g p pfg: isEqualizer f g p pfg
∑ a : enriched_equalizer_cone (self_enrichment V) f g,
is_equalizer_enriched (self_enrichment V) f g a

    exact (self_enrichment_equalizer_cone p pfg
           ,,
           self_enrichment_equalizer_is_equalizer p pfg H).
  Defined.

  (**
   4. Powers

  Section SelfEnrichmentPower.
    Context (v₁ v₂ : V).

V

V
 exact (v₁ ⊸ v₂).

 exact (internal_lam (sym_mon_braiding _ _ _ · internal_eval v₁ v₂)).
    Defined.

  self_enrichment_power_cone w

  (self_enrichment V ⦃ w, self_enrichment_power_cone ⦄)

V: sym_mon_closed_cat
v₁, v₂, w, a₁: V
h₁: V ⟦ a₁, w ⟧
a₂: V
h₂: V ⟦ a₂, v₁ ⟧
is_power_enriched_map (self_enrichment V) v₁ v₂
  self_enrichment_power_cone w
#⊗ (sym_mon_braiding V a₁ a₂ · h₂ #⊗ h₁)
· mon_rassociator (v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂) v₁ w
· internal_eval v₁ (w ⊸ v₂) #⊗ identity w
· internal_eval w v₂ = ?t2

h₁: V ⟦ a₁, w ⟧
a₂: V
h₂: V ⟦ a₂, v₁ ⟧
identity
  (self_enrichment V ⦃ w, self_enrichment_power_cone ⦄)
#⊗ sym_mon_braiding V a₁ a₂
· is_power_enriched_map (self_enrichment V) v₁ v₂
    self_enrichment_power_cone w #⊗ (h₂ #⊗ h₁)
· mon_rassociator (v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂) v₁ w
· internal_eval v₁ (w ⊸ v₂) #⊗ identity w
· internal_eval w v₂ = ?t2

#⊗ sym_mon_braiding V a₁ a₂
· (is_power_enriched_map (self_enrichment V) v₁ v₂
     self_enrichment_power_cone w #⊗ (h₂ #⊗ h₁)

         · internal_eval w v₂))) = ?t2

internal_lam
  (identity
     (self_enrichment V ⦃ w,
      self_enrichment_power_cone ⦄)
   #⊗ power_cone_mor (self_enrichment V) v₁ v₂
        self_enrichment_power_cone

        ⦃ self_enrichment_power_cone, v₂ ⦄)
   · enriched_comp (self_enrichment V) w
       self_enrichment_power_cone v₂) #⊗ identity v₁
· internal_eval v₁ (w ⊸ v₂) = ?t2

V: sym_mon_closed_cat
v₁, v₂, w, a₁: V
h₁: V ⟦ a₁, w ⟧
a₂: V
h₂: V ⟦ a₂, v₁ ⟧
mon_lassociator
  (self_enrichment V ⦃ w, self_enrichment_power_cone ⦄)
  a₁ a₂
· (identity
     (self_enrichment V ⦃ w,
      self_enrichment_power_cone ⦄)
   #⊗ sym_mon_braiding V a₁ a₂
   · (mon_rassociator
        (self_enrichment V ⦃ w,
         self_enrichment_power_cone ⦄) a₂ a₁
      · ((identity
            (self_enrichment V ⦃ w,
             self_enrichment_power_cone ⦄) #⊗ h₂
          · (identity
               (self_enrichment V ⦃ w,
                self_enrichment_power_cone ⦄)
             #⊗ power_cone_mor (self_enrichment V) v₁
                  v₂ self_enrichment_power_cone
             · sym_mon_braiding V
                 (self_enrichment V ⦃ w,
                  self_enrichment_power_cone ⦄)
                 (self_enrichment V
                  ⦃ self_enrichment_power_cone, v₂ ⦄)
             · enriched_comp (self_enrichment V) w
                 self_enrichment_power_cone v₂)) #⊗ h₁
         · internal_eval w v₂))) =
(identity
   (self_enrichment V ⦃ w, self_enrichment_power_cone
    ⦄) #⊗ h₁ · internal_eval w (v₁ ⊸ v₂)) #⊗ h₂
· internal_eval v₁ v₂

             · internal_comp w (v₁ ⊸ v₂) v₂)) #⊗ h₁
         · internal_eval w v₂))) =

 · internal_eval w (v₁ ⊸ v₂)) #⊗ h₂
· internal_eval v₁ v₂

   · (mon_rassociator (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) a₂ a₁
      · ((identity (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) #⊗ h₂
          · (identity (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂)
             #⊗ internal_lam
                  (sym_mon_braiding V v₁ (v₁ ⊸ v₂)
                   · internal_eval v₁ v₂)
             · sym_mon_braiding V (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂)
                 ((v₁ ⊸ v₂) ⊸ v₂))) #⊗ h₁
         · (mon_lassociator ((v₁ ⊸ v₂) ⊸ v₂)

            · (identity ((v₁ ⊸ v₂) ⊸ v₂)

(identity (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) #⊗ h₁

· internal_eval v₁ v₂

   · (mon_rassociator (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) a₂ a₁
      · ((identity (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) #⊗ h₂
          · (identity (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂)
             #⊗ internal_lam
                  (sym_mon_braiding V v₁ (v₁ ⊸ v₂)
                   · internal_eval v₁ v₂)
             · sym_mon_braiding V (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂)
                 ((v₁ ⊸ v₂) ⊸ v₂))) #⊗ h₁
         · (mon_lassociator ((v₁ ⊸ v₂) ⊸ v₂)
              (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) w
            · (identity ((v₁ ⊸ v₂) ⊸ v₂)
               #⊗ internal_eval w (v₁ ⊸ v₂)
               · internal_eval (v₁ ⊸ v₂) v₂))))) = 
?b

mon_lassociator (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) a₁ a₂
· identity (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) #⊗ sym_mon_braiding V a₁ a₂
· mon_rassociator (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) a₂ a₁
· (identity (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) #⊗ h₂) #⊗ h₁
· sym_mon_braiding V (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) v₁ #⊗ identity w
· mon_lassociator v₁ (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) w
· identity v₁ #⊗ internal_eval w (v₁ ⊸ v₂)
· sym_mon_braiding V v₁ (v₁ ⊸ v₂) = ?b

        
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
v₁, v₂, w, a₁: V
h₁: V ⟦ a₁, w ⟧
a₂: V
h₂: V ⟦ a₂, v₁ ⟧
mon_lassociator (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) a₁ a₂
· identity (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) #⊗ sym_mon_braiding V a₁ a₂
· mon_rassociator (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) a₂ a₁
· (identity (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) #⊗ h₂) #⊗ h₁ = ?y'

        
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
v₁, v₂, w, a₁: V
h₁: V ⟦ a₁, w ⟧
a₂: V
h₂: V ⟦ a₂, v₁ ⟧
mon_lassociator (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) a₁ a₂
· (identity (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) #⊗ sym_mon_braiding V a₁ a₂
   · (mon_rassociator (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) a₂ a₁
      · (identity (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) #⊗ h₂) #⊗ h₁)) = ?y'

        
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
v₁, v₂, w, a₁: V
h₁: V ⟦ a₁, w ⟧
a₂: V
h₂: V ⟦ a₂, v₁ ⟧
mon_lassociator (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) a₁ a₂
· (identity (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) #⊗ sym_mon_braiding V a₁ a₂
   · (identity (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) #⊗ (h₂ #⊗ h₁)
      · mon_rassociator (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) v₁ w)) = ?y'

        
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
v₁, v₂, w, a₁: V
h₁: V ⟦ a₁, w ⟧
a₂: V

· identity (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) #⊗ (h₂ #⊗ h₁)
· mon_rassociator (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) v₁ w = ?y'

· identity (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) #⊗ (h₂ #⊗ h₁) = ?y'

        
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
v₁, v₂, w, a₁: V

mon_lassociator (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) a₁ a₂

   · identity (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) #⊗ (h₂ #⊗ h₁)) = ?y'

· identity (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂)
  #⊗ (sym_mon_braiding V a₁ a₂ · h₂ #⊗ h₁) = ?y'

· identity (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂)
  #⊗ (h₁ #⊗ h₂ · sym_mon_braiding V w v₁) = ?y'

· mon_lassociator (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) w v₁ = ?y'

        apply idpath.
      
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
v₁, v₂, w, a₁: V
h₁: V ⟦ a₁, w ⟧
a₂: V
h₂: V ⟦ a₂, v₁ ⟧
(identity (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) #⊗ h₁) #⊗ identity a₂
· identity ((w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) ⊗ w) #⊗ h₂
· mon_lassociator (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) w v₁
· identity (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) #⊗ sym_mon_braiding V w v₁
· mon_rassociator (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) v₁ w
· sym_mon_braiding V (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) v₁ #⊗ identity w
· mon_lassociator v₁ (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) w
· identity v₁ #⊗ internal_eval w (v₁ ⊸ v₂)
· sym_mon_braiding V v₁ (v₁ ⊸ v₂) =
(identity (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) #⊗ h₁
 · internal_eval w (v₁ ⊸ v₂)) #⊗ h₂

      
V: sym_mon_closed_cat

a₂: V
h₂: V ⟦ a₂, v₁ ⟧
(identity (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) #⊗ h₁) #⊗ identity a₂
· (identity ((w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) ⊗ w) #⊗ h₂
   · (mon_lassociator (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) w v₁
      · (identity (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂)
         #⊗ sym_mon_braiding V w v₁
         · (mon_rassociator (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) v₁ w

                     #⊗ internal_eval w (v₁ ⊸ v₂)
                     · sym_mon_braiding V v₁ (v₁ ⊸ v₂)))))))) =

 · internal_eval w (v₁ ⊸ v₂)) #⊗ h₂

· (identity (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) #⊗ sym_mon_braiding V w v₁
   · (mon_rassociator (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) v₁ w
      · (sym_mon_braiding V (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) v₁
         #⊗ identity w
         · (mon_lassociator v₁ (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) w
            · (sym_mon_braiding V v₁
                 ((w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) ⊗ w)
               · internal_eval w (v₁ ⊸ v₂)
                 #⊗ identity v₁))))) =
identity ((w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) ⊗ w ⊗ v₁)
· internal_eval w (v₁ ⊸ v₂) #⊗ identity v₁

      
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
v₁, v₂, w, a₁: V

a₂: V

· identity (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) #⊗ sym_mon_braiding V w v₁

· sym_mon_braiding V v₁ ((w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) ⊗ w)
· internal_eval w (v₁ ⊸ v₂) #⊗ identity v₁ =
identity ((w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) ⊗ w ⊗ v₁)
· internal_eval w (v₁ ⊸ v₂) #⊗ identity v₁

      
V: sym_mon_closed_cat

· sym_mon_braiding V (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) v₁ #⊗ identity w

· sym_mon_braiding V v₁ ((w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) ⊗ w) =

V: sym_mon_closed_cat
v₁, v₂, w, a₁: V

a₂: V

mon_lassociator (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) w v₁
· identity (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) #⊗ sym_mon_braiding V w v₁
· mon_rassociator (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) v₁ w
· sym_mon_braiding V (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) v₁ #⊗ identity w
· mon_lassociator v₁ (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) w
· sym_mon_braiding V v₁ ((w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) ⊗ w)
· identity ((w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) ⊗ w ⊗ v₁) =
identity ((w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) ⊗ w ⊗ v₁)

      
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
v₁, v₂, w, a₁: V
h₁: V ⟦ a₁, w ⟧
a₂: V
h₂: V ⟦ a₂, v₁ ⟧
mon_lassociator (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) w v₁
· (identity (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) #⊗ sym_mon_braiding V w v₁
   · (mon_rassociator (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) v₁ w
      · (sym_mon_braiding V (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) v₁
         #⊗ identity w
         · (mon_lassociator v₁ (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) w
            · (sym_mon_braiding V v₁
                 ((w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) ⊗ w)
               · identity ((w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) ⊗ w ⊗ v₁)))))) =
identity ((w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) ⊗ w ⊗ v₁)

      
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
v₁, v₂, w, a₁: V
h₁: V ⟦ a₁, w ⟧
a₂: V
h₂: V ⟦ a₂, v₁ ⟧
mon_lassociator (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) w v₁
· (identity (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) #⊗ sym_mon_braiding V w v₁
   · (mon_rassociator (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) v₁ w
      · (sym_mon_braiding V (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) v₁
         #⊗ identity w
         · (mon_lassociator v₁ (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) w
            · (sym_mon_braiding V v₁
                 ((w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) ⊗ w)
               · (mon_lassociator (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) w v₁
                  · mon_rassociator (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) w v₁)))))) =
mon_lassociator (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) w v₁
· mon_rassociator (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) w v₁

      
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
v₁, v₂, w, a₁: V
h₁: V ⟦ a₁, w ⟧
a₂: V
h₂: V ⟦ a₂, v₁ ⟧
identity (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) #⊗ sym_mon_braiding V w v₁
· (mon_rassociator (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) v₁ w
   · (sym_mon_braiding V (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) v₁
      #⊗ identity w
      · (mon_lassociator v₁ (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) w
         · (sym_mon_braiding V v₁ ((w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) ⊗ w)
            · (mon_lassociator (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) w v₁
               · mon_rassociator (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) w v₁))))) =
mon_rassociator (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) w v₁

   · mon_rassociator (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) w v₁) =

· identity (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) #⊗ sym_mon_braiding V v₁ w
· mon_rassociator (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) w v₁ =

a₂: V

identity (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂)
#⊗ (sym_mon_braiding V w v₁ · sym_mon_braiding V v₁ w)
· mon_rassociator (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) w v₁ =
mon_rassociator (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) w v₁

      
V: sym_mon_closed_cat

· mon_rassociator (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) w v₁ =
mon_rassociator (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) w v₁

a₂: V

identity ((w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) ⊗ (w ⊗ v₁))
· mon_rassociator (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) w v₁ =
mon_rassociator (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) w v₁

      apply id_left.
    Qed.

    
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
v₁, v₂, w: V
internal_swap_arg v₁ v₂ w
· is_power_enriched_map (self_enrichment V) v₁ v₂
    self_enrichment_power_cone w =
identity (v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂)

    
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
v₁, v₂, w: V
internal_swap_arg v₁ v₂ w
· is_power_enriched_map (self_enrichment V) v₁ v₂
    self_enrichment_power_cone w =
identity (v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂)

      
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
v₁, v₂, w: V
∏ (a : V) (h : V ⟦ a, v₁ ⟧),
(internal_swap_arg v₁ v₂ w
 · is_power_enriched_map (self_enrichment V) v₁ v₂
     self_enrichment_power_cone w) #⊗ h
· internal_eval v₁ (self_enrichment V ⦃ w, v₂ ⦄) =
identity (v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂) #⊗ h
· internal_eval v₁ (self_enrichment V ⦃ w, v₂ ⦄)

      
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
v₁, v₂, w, a₁: V
h₁: V ⟦ a₁, v₁ ⟧
(internal_swap_arg v₁ v₂ w
 · is_power_enriched_map (self_enrichment V) v₁ v₂
     self_enrichment_power_cone w) #⊗ h₁
· internal_eval v₁ (self_enrichment V ⦃ w, v₂ ⦄) =
identity (v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂) #⊗ h₁
· internal_eval v₁ (self_enrichment V ⦃ w, v₂ ⦄)

      
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
v₁, v₂, w, a₁: V
h₁: V ⟦ a₁, v₁ ⟧
internal_swap_arg v₁ v₂ w #⊗ h₁
· is_power_enriched_map (self_enrichment V) v₁ v₂
    self_enrichment_power_cone w #⊗ identity v₁
· internal_eval v₁ (self_enrichment V ⦃ w, v₂ ⦄) =
identity (v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂) #⊗ h₁
· internal_eval v₁ (self_enrichment V ⦃ w, v₂ ⦄)

      
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
v₁, v₂, w, a₁: V
h₁: V ⟦ a₁, v₁ ⟧
internal_swap_arg v₁ v₂ w #⊗ h₁
· internal_lam
    (identity
       (self_enrichment V ⦃ w,
        self_enrichment_power_cone ⦄)
     #⊗ power_cone_mor (self_enrichment V) v₁ v₂
          self_enrichment_power_cone
     · sym_mon_braiding V
         (self_enrichment V ⦃ w,
          self_enrichment_power_cone ⦄)
         (self_enrichment V
          ⦃ self_enrichment_power_cone, v₂ ⦄)
     · enriched_comp (self_enrichment V) w
         self_enrichment_power_cone v₂) #⊗ identity v₁
· internal_eval v₁ (self_enrichment V ⦃ w, v₂ ⦄) =
identity (v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂) #⊗ h₁
· internal_eval v₁ (self_enrichment V ⦃ w, v₂ ⦄)

      
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
v₁, v₂, w, a₁: V
h₁: V ⟦ a₁, v₁ ⟧
internal_swap_arg v₁ v₂ w #⊗ h₁
· (internal_lam
     (identity
        (self_enrichment V ⦃ w,
         self_enrichment_power_cone ⦄)
      #⊗ power_cone_mor (self_enrichment V) v₁ v₂
           self_enrichment_power_cone
      · (sym_mon_braiding V
           (self_enrichment V ⦃ w,
            self_enrichment_power_cone ⦄)
           (self_enrichment V
            ⦃ self_enrichment_power_cone, v₂ ⦄)
         · enriched_comp (self_enrichment V) w
             self_enrichment_power_cone v₂))
   #⊗ identity v₁
   · internal_eval v₁ (self_enrichment V ⦃ w, v₂ ⦄)) =
identity (v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂) #⊗ h₁
· internal_eval v₁ (self_enrichment V ⦃ w, v₂ ⦄)

      
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
v₁, v₂, w, a₁: V
h₁: V ⟦ a₁, v₁ ⟧
internal_swap_arg v₁ v₂ w #⊗ h₁
· (identity (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂)
   #⊗ internal_lam
        (sym_mon_braiding V v₁ (v₁ ⊸ v₂)
         · internal_eval v₁ v₂)
   · (sym_mon_braiding V (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂)
        ((v₁ ⊸ v₂) ⊸ v₂)
      · internal_comp w (v₁ ⊸ v₂) v₂)) =
identity (v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂) #⊗ h₁
· internal_eval v₁ (w ⊸ v₂)

      
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
v₁, v₂, w, a₁: V
h₁: V ⟦ a₁, v₁ ⟧
∏ (a : V) (h : V ⟦ a, w ⟧),
(internal_swap_arg v₁ v₂ w #⊗ h₁
 · (identity (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂)
    #⊗ internal_lam
         (sym_mon_braiding V v₁ (v₁ ⊸ v₂)
          · internal_eval v₁ v₂)
    · (sym_mon_braiding V (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂)
         ((v₁ ⊸ v₂) ⊸ v₂)
       · internal_comp w (v₁ ⊸ v₂) v₂))) #⊗ h
· internal_eval w v₂ =
(identity (v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂) #⊗ h₁
 · internal_eval v₁ (w ⊸ v₂)) #⊗ h
· internal_eval w v₂

      
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
v₁, v₂, w, a₁: V
h₁: V ⟦ a₁, v₁ ⟧
a₂: V
h₂: V ⟦ a₂, w ⟧
(internal_swap_arg v₁ v₂ w #⊗ h₁
 · (identity (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂)
    #⊗ internal_lam
         (sym_mon_braiding V v₁ (v₁ ⊸ v₂)
          · internal_eval v₁ v₂)
    · (sym_mon_braiding V (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂)
         ((v₁ ⊸ v₂) ⊸ v₂)
       · internal_comp w (v₁ ⊸ v₂) v₂))) #⊗ h₂
· internal_eval w v₂ =
(identity (v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂) #⊗ h₁
 · internal_eval v₁ (w ⊸ v₂)) #⊗ h₂
· internal_eval w v₂

      
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
v₁, v₂, w, a₁: V
h₁: V ⟦ a₁, v₁ ⟧
a₂: V
h₂: V ⟦ a₂, w ⟧
(internal_swap_arg v₁ v₂ w #⊗ h₁) #⊗ h₂
· ((identity (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂)
    #⊗ internal_lam
         (sym_mon_braiding V v₁ (v₁ ⊸ v₂)
          · internal_eval v₁ v₂)) #⊗ identity w
   · (sym_mon_braiding V (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂)
        ((v₁ ⊸ v₂) ⊸ v₂) #⊗ identity w
      · internal_comp w (v₁ ⊸ v₂) v₂ #⊗ identity w))
· internal_eval w v₂ =
(identity (v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂) #⊗ h₁) #⊗ h₂
· internal_eval v₁ (w ⊸ v₂) #⊗ identity w
· internal_eval w v₂

      
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
v₁, v₂, w, a₁: V
h₁: V ⟦ a₁, v₁ ⟧
a₂: V
h₂: V ⟦ a₂, w ⟧
(internal_swap_arg v₁ v₂ w #⊗ h₁) #⊗ h₂
· ((identity (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂)
    #⊗ internal_lam
         (sym_mon_braiding V v₁ (v₁ ⊸ v₂)
          · internal_eval v₁ v₂)) #⊗ identity w
   · (sym_mon_braiding V (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂)
        ((v₁ ⊸ v₂) ⊸ v₂) #⊗ identity w
      · (internal_comp w (v₁ ⊸ v₂) v₂ #⊗ identity w
         · internal_eval w v₂))) =
(identity (v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂) #⊗ h₁) #⊗ h₂
· (internal_eval v₁ (w ⊸ v₂) #⊗ identity w
   · internal_eval w v₂)

a₂: V

   · (sym_mon_braiding V (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂)

      · (internal_lam
           (mon_lassociator ((v₁ ⊸ v₂) ⊸ v₂)
              (w ⊸ v₁ ⊸ v₂) w
            · identity ((v₁ ⊸ v₂) ⊸ v₂)
              #⊗ internal_eval w (v₁ ⊸ v₂)
            · internal_eval (v₁ ⊸ v₂) v₂)
         #⊗ identity w · internal_eval w v₂))) =
(identity (v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂) #⊗ h₁) #⊗ h₂
· (internal_eval v₁ (w ⊸ v₂) #⊗ identity w
   · internal_eval w v₂)

· (internal_eval w (v₁ ⊸ v₂) #⊗ identity v₁
   · internal_eval v₁ v₂) = ?t2

        apply idpath.

   · internal_eval w v₂)

V: sym_mon_closed_cat

   · (mon_lassociator a₁ (v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂) w
      · (sym_mon_braiding V a₁ ((v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂) ⊗ w)
         · (identity ((v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂) ⊗ w) #⊗ h₁
            · (mon_lassociator (v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂) w v₁
               · (identity (v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂)
                  #⊗ sym_mon_braiding V w v₁
                  · (mon_rassociator (v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂) v₁
                       w
                     · (internal_eval v₁ (w ⊸ v₂)
                        #⊗ identity w
                        · internal_eval w v₂)))))))) =

V: sym_mon_closed_cat
v₁, v₂, w, a₁: V
h₁: V ⟦ a₁, v₁ ⟧
a₂: V
h₂: V ⟦ a₂, w ⟧
identity ((v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂) ⊗ a₁) #⊗ h₂
· sym_mon_braiding V (v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂) a₁ #⊗ identity w
· mon_lassociator a₁ (v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂) w
· sym_mon_braiding V a₁ ((v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂) ⊗ w)
· identity ((v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂) ⊗ w) #⊗ h₁
· mon_lassociator (v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂) w v₁
· identity (v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂) #⊗ sym_mon_braiding V w v₁
· mon_rassociator (v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂) v₁ w
· internal_eval v₁ (w ⊸ v₂) #⊗ identity w
· internal_eval w v₂ =
(identity (v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂) #⊗ h₁) #⊗ h₂
· internal_eval v₁ (w ⊸ v₂) #⊗ identity w
· internal_eval w v₂

      
V: sym_mon_closed_cat

h₁: V ⟦ a₁, v₁ ⟧
a₂: V
h₂: V ⟦ a₂, w ⟧
identity ((v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂) ⊗ a₁) #⊗ h₂
· sym_mon_braiding V (v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂) a₁ #⊗ identity w
· mon_lassociator a₁ (v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂) w
· sym_mon_braiding V a₁ ((v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂) ⊗ w)
· identity ((v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂) ⊗ w) #⊗ h₁
· mon_lassociator (v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂) w v₁
· identity (v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂) #⊗ sym_mon_braiding V w v₁
· mon_rassociator (v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂) v₁ w =
(identity (v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂) #⊗ h₁) #⊗ h₂

      
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
v₁, v₂, w, a₁: V
h₁: V ⟦ a₁, v₁ ⟧
a₂: V
h₂: V ⟦ a₂, w ⟧
identity ((v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂) ⊗ a₁) #⊗ h₂
· sym_mon_braiding V (v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂) a₁ #⊗ identity w
· mon_lassociator a₁ (v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂) w
· sym_mon_braiding V a₁ ((v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂) ⊗ w)
· identity ((v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂) ⊗ w) #⊗ h₁
· mon_lassociator (v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂) w v₁
· identity (v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂) #⊗ sym_mon_braiding V w v₁
· mon_rassociator (v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂) v₁ w = ?b
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
v₁, v₂, w, a₁: V
h₁: V ⟦ a₁, v₁ ⟧
a₂: V
h₂: V ⟦ a₂, w ⟧
?b = (identity (v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂) #⊗ h₁) #⊗ h₂

      
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
v₁, v₂, w, a₁: V
h₁: V ⟦ a₁, v₁ ⟧
a₂: V
h₂: V ⟦ a₂, w ⟧
identity ((v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂) ⊗ a₁) #⊗ h₂
· sym_mon_braiding V (v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂) a₁ #⊗ identity w
· mon_lassociator a₁ (v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂) w
· sym_mon_braiding V a₁ ((v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂) ⊗ w)
· identity ((v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂) ⊗ w) #⊗ h₁
· mon_lassociator (v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂) w v₁
· identity (v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂) #⊗ sym_mon_braiding V w v₁
· mon_rassociator (v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂) v₁ w = ?b

h₁: V ⟦ a₁, v₁ ⟧
a₂: V
h₂: V ⟦ a₂, w ⟧
identity ((v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂) ⊗ a₁) #⊗ h₂
· sym_mon_braiding V (v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂) a₁ #⊗ identity w
· mon_lassociator a₁ (v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂) w
· sym_mon_braiding V a₁ ((v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂) ⊗ w)
· identity ((v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂) ⊗ w) #⊗ h₁ = ?y'

a₂: V

· mon_rassociator (v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂) v₁ w = ?t20

          
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
v₁, v₂, w, a₁: V
h₁: V ⟦ a₁, v₁ ⟧
a₂: V
h₂: V ⟦ a₂, w ⟧
identity (v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂)
#⊗ (sym_mon_braiding V v₁ w · sym_mon_braiding V w v₁)
· mon_rassociator (v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂) v₁ w = ?t20

          
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
v₁, v₂, w, a₁: V
h₁: V ⟦ a₁, v₁ ⟧
a₂: V
h₂: V ⟦ a₂, w ⟧
identity (v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂) #⊗ identity (v₁ ⊗ w)
· mon_rassociator (v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂) v₁ w = ?t20

          
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
v₁, v₂, w, a₁: V
h₁: V ⟦ a₁, v₁ ⟧
a₂: V
h₂: V ⟦ a₂, w ⟧
identity ((v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂) ⊗ (v₁ ⊗ w))
· mon_rassociator (v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂) v₁ w = ?t20

          apply id_left.
        
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
v₁, v₂, w, a₁: V
h₁: V ⟦ a₁, v₁ ⟧
a₂: V
h₂: V ⟦ a₂, w ⟧
sym_mon_braiding V v₁ (v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂) #⊗ identity w
· (mon_lassociator (v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂) v₁ w
   · mon_rassociator (v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂) v₁ w) = ?t2

        
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
v₁, v₂, w, a₁: V
h₁: V ⟦ a₁, v₁ ⟧
a₂: V
h₂: V ⟦ a₂, w ⟧
sym_mon_braiding V v₁ (v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂) #⊗ identity w
· identity ((v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂) ⊗ v₁ ⊗ w) = ?t2

        apply id_right.
      
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
v₁, v₂, w, a₁: V
h₁: V ⟦ a₁, v₁ ⟧
a₂: V
h₂: V ⟦ a₂, w ⟧
sym_mon_braiding V (v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂) v₁ #⊗ identity w
· sym_mon_braiding V v₁ (v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂) #⊗ identity w =
identity ((v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂) ⊗ v₁ ⊗ w)

      
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
v₁, v₂, w, a₁: V
h₁: V ⟦ a₁, v₁ ⟧
a₂: V
h₂: V ⟦ a₂, w ⟧
(sym_mon_braiding V (v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂) v₁
 · sym_mon_braiding V v₁ (v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂)) #⊗ identity w =
identity ((v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂) ⊗ v₁ ⊗ w)

      
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
v₁, v₂, w, a₁: V
h₁: V ⟦ a₁, v₁ ⟧
a₂: V
h₂: V ⟦ a₂, w ⟧
identity ((v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂) ⊗ v₁) #⊗ identity w =
identity ((v₁ ⊸ w ⊸ v₂) ⊗ v₁ ⊗ w)

      apply tensor_id_id.
    Qed.

    
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
v₁, v₂: V
is_power_enriched (self_enrichment V) v₁ v₂
  self_enrichment_power_cone

    
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
v₁, v₂: V
is_power_enriched (self_enrichment V) v₁ v₂
  self_enrichment_power_cone

      
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
v₁, v₂: V
∏ w : V,
V ⟦ v₁ ⊸ (self_enrichment V ⦃ w, v₂ ⦄),
self_enrichment V ⦃ w, self_enrichment_power_cone ⦄ ⟧
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
v₁, v₂: V
∏ w : V,
is_power_enriched_map (self_enrichment V) v₁ v₂
  self_enrichment_power_cone w · ?p_map w =
identity
  (self_enrichment V ⦃ w, self_enrichment_power_cone ⦄)
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
v₁, v₂: V
∏ w : V,
?p_map w
· is_power_enriched_map (self_enrichment V) v₁ v₂
    self_enrichment_power_cone w =
identity (v₁ ⊸ (self_enrichment V ⦃ w, v₂ ⦄))

      
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
v₁, v₂: V
∏ w : V,
V ⟦ v₁ ⊸ (self_enrichment V ⦃ w, v₂ ⦄),
self_enrichment V ⦃ w, self_enrichment_power_cone ⦄ ⟧
 exact (λ w, internal_swap_arg v₁ v₂ w).
      
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
v₁, v₂: V
∏ w : V,
is_power_enriched_map (self_enrichment V) v₁ v₂
  self_enrichment_power_cone w
· (λ w0 : V, internal_swap_arg v₁ v₂ w0) w =
identity
  (self_enrichment V ⦃ w, self_enrichment_power_cone ⦄)
 exact is_power_self_enrichment_power_cone_eq_1.
      
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
v₁, v₂: V
∏ w : V,
(λ w0 : V, internal_swap_arg v₁ v₂ w0) w
· is_power_enriched_map (self_enrichment V) v₁ v₂
    self_enrichment_power_cone w =
identity (v₁ ⊸ (self_enrichment V ⦃ w, v₂ ⦄))
 exact is_power_self_enrichment_power_cone_eq_2.
    Defined.
  End SelfEnrichmentPower.

  Definition self_enrichment_powers
    : enrichment_power (self_enrichment V)
    := λ v₁ v₂,
      self_enrichment_power_cone v₁ v₂
      ,,
      is_power_self_enrichment_power_cone v₁ v₂.

  (**
   5. Type indexed products
   *)
  Section SelfEnrichmentProduct.
    Context {J : UU}
            {D : J → V}
            (prod : Product J V D).

    
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
J: UU
D: J → V
prod: Product J V D
enriched_prod_cone (self_enrichment V) D

    
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
J: UU
D: J → V
prod: Product J V D
enriched_prod_cone (self_enrichment V) D

      
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
J: UU
D: J → V
prod: Product J V D
V
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
J: UU
D: J → V
prod: Product J V D
∏ j : J, V ⟦ I_{ V}, self_enrichment V ⦃ ?a, D j ⦄ ⟧

      
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
J: UU
D: J → V
prod: Product J V D
V
 exact prod.
      
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
J: UU
D: J → V
prod: Product J V D
∏ j : J, V ⟦ I_{ V}, self_enrichment V ⦃ prod, D j ⦄ ⟧
 exact (λ j,
               enriched_from_arr
                 (self_enrichment V)
                 (ProductPr _ _ prod j)).
    Defined.

    
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
J: UU
D: J → V
prod: Product J V D
is_prod_enriched (self_enrichment V) D
  self_enrichment_prod_cone

    
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
J: UU
D: J → V
prod: Product J V D
is_prod_enriched (self_enrichment V) D
  self_enrichment_prod_cone

      
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
J: UU
D: J → V
prod: Product J V D
∏ w v : V,
(∏ j : J, V ⟦ v, self_enrichment V ⦃ w, D j ⦄ ⟧)
→ V ⟦ v,
  self_enrichment V ⦃ w, self_enrichment_prod_cone ⦄ ⟧
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
J: UU
D: J → V
prod: Product J V D
∏ (w v : V)
(f : ∏ j : J, V ⟦ v, self_enrichment V ⦃ w, D j ⦄ ⟧)
(j : J),
?pair w v f
· postcomp_arr (self_enrichment V) w
    (enriched_prod_cone_pr 
       (self_enrichment V) D self_enrichment_prod_cone
       j) = f j
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
J: UU
D: J → V
prod: Product J V D
∏ (w v : V)
(φ₁
 φ₂ : V ⟦ v,
      self_enrichment V ⦃ w, self_enrichment_prod_cone
      ⦄ ⟧),
(∏ j : J,
 φ₁
 · postcomp_arr (self_enrichment V) w
     (enriched_prod_cone_pr 
        (self_enrichment V) D
        self_enrichment_prod_cone j) =
 φ₂
 · postcomp_arr (self_enrichment V) w
     (enriched_prod_cone_pr 
        (self_enrichment V) D
        self_enrichment_prod_cone j)) → 
φ₁ = φ₂

      
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
J: UU
D: J → V
prod: Product J V D
∏ w v : V,
(∏ j : J, V ⟦ v, self_enrichment V ⦃ w, D j ⦄ ⟧)
→ V ⟦ v,
  self_enrichment V ⦃ w, self_enrichment_prod_cone ⦄ ⟧
 exact (λ v₁ v₂ f,
               internal_lam
                 (ProductArrow
                    _ _
                    prod
                    (λ j, f j #⊗ identity _ · internal_eval _ _))).
      
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
J: UU
D: J → V
prod: Product J V D
∏ (w v : V)
(f : ∏ j : J, V ⟦ v, self_enrichment V ⦃ w, D j ⦄ ⟧)
(j : J),
(λ (v₁ v₂ : V)
 (f0 : ∏ j0 : J,
       V ⟦ v₂, self_enrichment V ⦃ v₁, D j0 ⦄ ⟧),
 internal_lam
   (ProductArrow J V prod
      (λ j0 : J,
       f0 j0 #⊗ identity v₁ · internal_eval v₁ (D j0))))
  w v f
· postcomp_arr (self_enrichment V) w
    (enriched_prod_cone_pr (self_enrichment V) D
       self_enrichment_prod_cone j) = f j
 abstract
          (intros v₁ v₂ f j ; cbn ;
           rewrite self_enrichment_postcomp ;
           use internal_funext ;
           intros a h ;
           rewrite tensor_comp_r_id_r ;
           rewrite !assoc' ;
           rewrite internal_beta ;
           rewrite tensor_split ;
           rewrite !assoc' ;
           rewrite !(maponpaths (λ z, _ · z) (assoc _ _ _)) ;
           rewrite internal_beta ;
           rewrite internal_to_from_arr ;
           rewrite ProductPrCommutes ;
           rewrite !assoc ;
           rewrite <- tensor_split ;
           apply idpath).
      
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
J: UU
D: J → V
prod: Product J V D
∏ (w v : V)
(φ₁
 φ₂ : V ⟦ v,
      self_enrichment V ⦃ w, self_enrichment_prod_cone
      ⦄ ⟧),
(∏ j : J,
 φ₁
 · postcomp_arr (self_enrichment V) w
     (enriched_prod_cone_pr (self_enrichment V) D
        self_enrichment_prod_cone j) =
 φ₂
 · postcomp_arr (self_enrichment V) w
     (enriched_prod_cone_pr (self_enrichment V) D
        self_enrichment_prod_cone j)) → φ₁ = φ₂
 abstract
          (intros v₁ v₂ φ₁ φ₂ p ; cbn in * ;
           use internal_funext ;
           intros a h ;
           use (ProductArrow_eq _ _ _ prod) ;
           intro j ;
           pose (q := maponpaths (λ z, z #⊗ identity _ · internal_eval _ _) (p j)) ;
           cbn in q ;
           rewrite !self_enrichment_postcomp in q ;
           rewrite !tensor_comp_id_r in q ;
           rewrite !assoc' in q ;
           rewrite !internal_beta in q ;
           rewrite !internal_to_from_arr in q ;
           rewrite (tensor_split φ₁ h) ;
           rewrite (tensor_split φ₂ h) ;
           rewrite !assoc' ;
           rewrite q ;
           apply idpath).
    Defined.
  End SelfEnrichmentProduct.

  Definition self_enrichment_prod
             (J : UU)
             (PV : Products J V)
    : enrichment_prod (self_enrichment V) J
    := λ D,
       self_enrichment_prod_cone (PV D)
       ,,
       self_enrichment_is_product (PV D).
End SelfEnrichmentLimits.
